The extension pauses all sort of window opening requests for user attention. You can either accept or deny a request. Multiple unique requests are shown in an array. If a websites requests a single URL more than once, a badge number will be shown indicating the total number of requests to this particular URL.\r\n\r\n\r\nPlease note that the extension is recently renamed from \"Popup Blocker (ultimate)\" to \"Popup Blocker (strict)\"\r\n\r\nOptions:\r\n1. In this transaction, money does not actually change hands until some agreed upon future date\r\nSwap Forex Trading - The most common type of forward transaction is the foreign exchange swap. The average contract length is roughly 3 months. Futures contracts are usually inclusive of any interest amounts.\r\nOption Trade - A foreign exchange option (commonly shortened to just FX option) is a derivative where the owner has the right but not the obligation to exchange money denominated in one currency into another currency at a pre-agreed exchange rate on a specified date.\r\nLibor - The London Interbank Offered Rate is the average interest rate estimated by leading banks in London that the average leading bank would be charged if borrowing from other banks. It is used as a reference in the forex market.\r\nForex Risk aversion - Risk aversion is a kind of trading behavior exhibited by the foreign exchange market when a potentially adverse event happens which may affect market conditions.
